2426Product Summary<!-- -->

2427:</p>

2428<div class="SingleAttribute_descriptionAttribute__1T7wm">

2429From the Precis collection, this single basin kitchen sink comes in white. Made of granite composite, this rectangular undermount sink measures 32" x 19" x 9.5".</div>

2435<div class="SingleAttribute_section__GJ3I7 undefined">

2436<p class="SingleAttribute_groupTitle__1P8qJ" style="margin-bottom:10px">

2437Product Description<!-- -->

2438:</p>

2439<div class="SingleAttribute_descriptionAttribute__1T7wm">

2440<p>

2441The Blanco Precis 32" Granite Single-Basin Kitchen sink is a large undermount sink made of white granite composite. Silgranit, a material that is 80% granite, is extra-durable and designed to prevent scratches, stains, and heat damage up to 536 degrees. The straightforward design includes a 9.5" basin depth, deep enough and wide enough to hold a wide array of dishes and pots and pans of various sizes.</p>

2442

2443<p>

2444<strong>

2445The Precis Collection</strong>

2446</p>

2447

2448<p>

2449The Precis collection from Blanco features sinks made of Silgranite, an 80% granite composite material designed to withstand scratches, stains, and heat up to 536 degrees. Sinks in the Precis collection are available in a wide range of colors, shapes, and sizes.</p>

2450

2451<p>

2452<strong>

2453Who is Blanco?</strong>

2454</p>

2455

2456<p>

2457For over 85 years, Blanco has produced quality sinks, faucets, and kitchen accessories for home remodel. A vast catalog includes the best materials, styles, and products to fit any budget. Blanco sinks include undermount, dual-mount, and drop-in install styles in addition to single and double-basin designs.</p>
